// Copyright (c) MudBlazor 2021
// MudBlazor licenses this file to you under the MIT license.
// See the LICENSE file in the project root for more information.

using System.Diagnostics.CodeAnalysis;
using MudBlazor.Extensions;
using MudBlazor.Interfaces;
using MudBlazor.Utilities;

namespace MudBlazor;

/// <summary>
/// Manages the communication between <see cref="MudSelect{T}"/> and <see cref="MudSelectItem{T}"/> components.
/// </summary>
/// <typeparam name="T">The type of value being selected.</typeparam>
internal sealed class MudSelectContext<T>
{
    private readonly MudSelect<T> _select;
    private readonly List<MudSelectItem<T>> _items = [];
    private readonly List<Func<IReadOnlyCollection<T?>, Task>> _selectionObservers = [];
    private readonly NullableObjectComparer _comparer;
    private Dictionary<NullableObject<T?>, MudSelectItem<T>> _valueLookup;
    private Dictionary<NullableObject<T?>, MudSelectItem<T>> _shadowLookup;

    /// <summary>
    /// Initializes a new instance of the <see cref="MudSelectContext{T}"/> class.
    /// </summary>
    /// <param name="select">The parent select component.</param>
    public MudSelectContext(MudSelect<T> select)
    {
        _select = select;
        _comparer = new NullableObjectComparer(select);
        _valueLookup = new Dictionary<NullableObject<T?>, MudSelectItem<T>>(_comparer);
        _shadowLookup = new Dictionary<NullableObject<T?>, MudSelectItem<T>>(_comparer);
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// An <see cref="IEqualityComparer{T}"/> for <see cref="NullableObject{T}"/> that delegates to the user-provided comparer.
    /// </summary>
    private sealed class NullableObjectComparer : IEqualityComparer<NullableObject<T?>>
    {
        private readonly MudSelect<T> _select;

        public NullableObjectComparer(MudSelect<T> select)
        {
            _select = select;
        }

        private IEqualityComparer<T?> ElementComparer => _select.Comparer ?? EqualityComparer<T?>.Default;

        public bool Equals(NullableObject<T?> x, NullableObject<T?> y)
        {
            if (x.IsNull && y.IsNull)
            {
                return true;
            }

            if (x.IsNull || y.IsNull)
            {
                return false;
            }

            return ElementComparer.Equals(x.Item, y.Item);
        }

        public int GetHashCode(NullableObject<T?> obj)
        {
            if (obj.IsNull)
            {
                return 0;
            }

            return ElementComparer.GetHashCode(obj.Item);
        }
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Gets the ordered list of all visible items in the dropdown.
    /// </summary>
    /// <remarks>
    /// Exposed as List to support FindIndex operations in the parent component.
    /// </remarks>
    public IReadOnlyList<MudSelectItem<T>> Items => _items;

    /// <summary>
    /// Gets all shadow items (including both visible and hidden items).
    /// </summary>
    public IReadOnlyCollection<MudSelectItem<T>> ShadowItems => _shadowLookup.Values;

    /// <summary>
    /// Gets whether multi-selection is enabled.
    /// </summary>
    public bool MultiSelection => _select.MultiSelection;

    /// <summary>
    /// Gets the current selected values.
    /// </summary>
    public IReadOnlyCollection<T?> SelectedValues => _select.GetSelectedValues() ?? Array.Empty<T?>();

    /// <summary>
    /// Gets the user-supplied value comparer from the parent <see cref="MudSelect{T}"/>, if any.
    /// </summary>
    public IEqualityComparer<T?>? Comparer => _select.Comparer;

    /// <summary>
    /// Rebuilds the internal dictionaries. This should be called when the comparer changes
    /// to ensure hash codes are recalculated with the new comparer.
    /// </summary>
    public void RebuildDictionaries()
    {
        // Rebuild value lookup with the current comparer
        var newValueLookup = new Dictionary<NullableObject<T?>, MudSelectItem<T>>(_comparer);
        foreach (var kvp in _valueLookup)
        {
            newValueLookup[kvp.Key] = kvp.Value;
        }
        _valueLookup = newValueLookup;

        // Rebuild shadow lookup with the current comparer
        var newShadowLookup = new Dictionary<NullableObject<T?>, MudSelectItem<T>>(_comparer);
        foreach (var kvp in _shadowLookup)
        {
            newShadowLookup[kvp.Key] = kvp.Value;
        }
        _shadowLookup = newShadowLookup;
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Registers an item as visible in the dropdown list.
    /// </summary>
    /// <param name="item">The item to register.</param>
    /// <returns><c>true</c> if the item is currently selected; otherwise <c>false</c>.</returns>
    public bool RegisterItem(MudSelectItem<T> item)
    {
        // Add to the ordered list of visible items
        if (!_items.Contains(item))
        {
            _items.Add(item);
        }

        // Add to value lookup for fast access by value
        _valueLookup[item.Value] = item;

        // Note: Do NOT add to _shadowLookup here - that's only for shadow items
        // Shadow items are registered separately via RegisterShadowItem

        // Check if this item's value is currently selected
        var comparer = _select.Comparer ?? EqualityComparer<T?>.Default;
        return _select.MultiSelection switch
        {
            true => _select.GetSelectedValues()?.Contains(item.Value, comparer) == true,
            false => comparer.Equals(_select.ReadValue, item.Value)
        };
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Unregisters an item from the dropdown list.
    /// </summary>
    /// <param name="item">The item to unregister.</param>
    public void UnregisterItem(MudSelectItem<T> item)
    {
        _items.Remove(item);
        _valueLookup.Remove(item.Value);
        // Note: Do NOT remove from _shadowLookup - that's managed by shadow items
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Registers an item for value-to-RenderFragment lookup only (not visible in dropdown).
    /// </summary>
    /// <remarks>
    /// Used for items with HideContent=true that provide RenderFragments for selected values
    /// that may not be in the visible dropdown list.
    /// </remarks>
    /// <param name="item">The item to register.</param>
    public void RegisterShadowItem(MudSelectItem<T>? item)
    {
        if (item is null)
        {
            return;
        }

        _shadowLookup[item.Value] = item;
        _select.InvalidateFitContent();
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Unregisters a shadow item.
    /// </summary>
    /// <param name="item">The item to unregister.</param>
    public void UnregisterShadowItem(MudSelectItem<T>? item)
    {
        if (item is null)
        {
            return;
        }

        _shadowLookup.Remove(item.Value);
        _select.InvalidateFitContent();
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Updates the visible-item lookup when a registered item's <see cref="MudSelectItem{T}.Value"/> parameter changes.
    /// </summary>
    /// <remarks>
    /// The lookup is keyed by value captured at registration time. When the value parameter is later mutated
    /// (e.g. the parent swaps the underlying data collection while reusing the same component instances),
    /// the old key would otherwise point to a stale <see cref="MudSelectItem{T}"/> reference and the new value
    /// would not be found at all.
    /// </remarks>
    public void OnItemValueChanged(MudSelectItem<T> item, T? oldValue, T? newValue)
    {
        var oldKey = new NullableObject<T?>(oldValue);
        if (_valueLookup.TryGetValue(oldKey, out var existing) && ReferenceEquals(existing, item))
        {
            _valueLookup.Remove(oldKey);
        }

        _valueLookup[newValue] = item;
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Updates the shadow lookup when a registered shadow item's <see cref="MudSelectItem{T}.Value"/> parameter changes.
    /// </summary>
    /// <remarks>
    /// Also requests a re-render of the parent <see cref="MudSelect{T}"/>: <c>GetSelectedValuePresenter</c> runs
    /// during the parent's render pass, before child <c>SetParametersAsync</c> has propagated the new value,
    /// so a second render is needed for the correct <see cref="MudSelectItem{T}.ChildContent"/> to be emitted.
    /// </remarks>
    public void OnShadowItemValueChanged(MudSelectItem<T> item, T? oldValue, T? newValue)
    {
        var oldKey = new NullableObject<T?>(oldValue);
        if (_shadowLookup.TryGetValue(oldKey, out var existing) && ReferenceEquals(existing, item))
        {
            _shadowLookup.Remove(oldKey);
        }

        _shadowLookup[newValue] = item;
        _select.InvalidateFitContent();
        ((IMudStateHasChanged)_select).StateHasChanged();
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Attempts to get an item by its value from visible items.
    /// </summary>
    public bool TryGetItemByValue(T? value, [NotNullWhen(true)] out MudSelectItem<T>? item)
    {
        return _valueLookup.TryGetValue(value, out item);
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Attempts to get an item by its value from all items (including shadow items).
    /// </summary>
    public bool TryGetShadowItemByValue(T? value, [NotNullWhen(true)] out MudSelectItem<T>? item)
    {
        return _shadowLookup.TryGetValue(value, out item);
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Subscribes to selection changes.
    /// </summary>
    /// <param name="observer">The callback to invoke when selection changes.</param>
    /// <returns>A disposable subscription that can be used to unsubscribe.</returns>
    public IDisposable SubscribeToSelectionChanges(Func<IReadOnlyCollection<T?>, Task> observer)
    {
        _selectionObservers.Add(observer);
        return new SelectionSubscription(this, observer);
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Unsubscribes an observer from selection changes.
    /// </summary>
    private void Unsubscribe(Func<IReadOnlyCollection<T?>, Task> observer)
    {
        _selectionObservers.Remove(observer);
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Notifies all observers of a selection change.
    /// </summary>
    public async Task NotifySelectionChangedAsync()
    {
        var selectedValues = SelectedValues;
        for (var i = _selectionObservers.Count - 1; i >= 0; i--)
        {
            await _selectionObservers[i](selectedValues);
        }
    }

    private sealed class SelectionSubscription(MudSelectContext<T> context, Func<IReadOnlyCollection<T?>, Task> observer)
        : IDisposable
    {
        private MudSelectContext<T>? _context = context;
        private Func<IReadOnlyCollection<T?>, Task>? _observer = observer;

        public void Dispose()
        {
            var contextCopy = _context;
            var observerCopy = _observer;

            if (contextCopy is null || observerCopy is null)
            {
                return;
            }

            _context = null;
            _observer = null;

            contextCopy.Unsubscribe(observerCopy);
        }
    }
}

Now let me think about edge cases I may have missed:

1. **Null values in dictionaries**: The `NullableObjectComparer` handles null values correctly - if both are null, they're equal; if only one is null, they're not equal.

2. **Comparer changes dynamically**: The `RebuildDictionaries` method is called from `OnComparerChangedAsync` to rebuild the dictionaries when the comparer changes. However, I should also check if there's an issue with `_selectedValues` being initialized without a comparer when both `Comparer` and `SelectedValues` are not set.

3. **Multiple levels of generic types**: The `NullableObject<T?>` where `T` is already nullable works correctly because the comparer is `IEqualityComparer<T?>`.

4. **The `MudSelectItem` registration flow**: When items register, they use `_valueLookup[item.Value] = item`, which now uses the custom comparer via `NullableObjectComparer`. The `RegisterItem` method also checks selection using the custom comparer.

Let me also check if there's any issue with `MudSelectItem`'s `OnSelectionChangedAsync`:

```csharp
private Task OnSelectionChangedAsync(IReadOnlyCollection<T?> selectedValues)
{
    var oldSelected = Selected;
    Selected = selectedValues.Contains(Value);
    ...
}
```

The `selectedValues` is `IReadOnlyCollection<T?>`. The LINQ `Contains` extension method checks if the collection implements `ICollection<T>` and uses its `Contains` method. Since the actual object is a `HashSet<T?>` created with the custom comparer, it will use the custom comparer for equality. This is correct.

But wait, what if someone casts the `HashSet<T?>` to `IReadOnlyCollection<T?>` and then calls `Contains`? Yes, that's exactly what happens. And as I explained, LINQ's `Contains` checks for `ICollection<T>` first. `HashSet<T>` implements `ICollection<T>`, so it uses `HashSet<T>.Contains` which respects the custom comparer.

Now, I'm fairly confident that my changes fix the issue. Let me also verify the final state of the two edited files:

     1	// Copyright (c) MudBlazor 2021

     4	
     5	using System.Diagnostics.CodeAnalysis;
     6	using MudBlazor.Extensions;
     7	using MudBlazor.Interfaces;
     8	using MudBlazor.Utilities;
     9	
    10	namespace MudBlazor;
    11	
    12	/// <summary>
    13	/// Manages the communication between <see cref="MudSelect{T}"/> and <see cref="MudSelectItem{T}"/> components.
    14	/// </summary>
    15	/// <typeparam name="T">The type of value being selected.</typeparam>
    16	internal sealed class MudSelectContext<T>
    17	{
    18	    private readonly MudSelect<T> _select;
    19	    private readonly List<MudSelectItem<T>> _items = [];
    20	    private readonly List<Func<IReadOnlyCollection<T?>, Task>> _selectionObservers = [];
    21	    private readonly NullableObjectComparer _comparer;
    22	    private Dictionary<NullableObject<T?>, MudSelectItem<T>> _valueLookup;
    23	    private Dictionary<NullableObject<T?>, MudSelectItem<T>> _shadowLookup;
    24	
    25	    /// <summary>
    26	    /// Initializes a new instance of the <see cref="MudSelectContext{T}"/> class.
    27	    /// </summary>
    28	    /// <param name="select">The parent select component.</param>
    29	    public MudSelectContext(MudSelect<T> select)
    30	    {
    31	        _select = select;
    32	        _comparer = new NullableObjectComparer(select);
    33	        _valueLookup = new Dictionary<NullableObject<T?>, MudSelectItem<T>>(_comparer);
    34	        _shadowLookup = new Dictionary<NullableObject<T?>, MudSelectItem<T>>(_comparer);
    35	    }
    36	
    37	    /// <summary>
    38	    /// An <see cref="IEqualityComparer{T}"/> for <see cref="NullableObject{T}"/> that delegates to the user-provided comparer.
    39	    /// </summary>
    40	    private sealed class NullableObjectComparer : IEqualityComparer<NullableObject<T?>>
    41	    {
    42	        private readonly MudSelect<T> _select;
    43	
    44	        public NullableObjectComparer(MudSelect<T> select)
    45	        {
    46	            _select = select;
    47	        }
    48	
    49	        private IEqualityComparer<T?> ElementComparer => _select.Comparer ?? EqualityComparer<T?>.Default;
    50	
    51	        public bool Equals(NullableObject<T?> x, NullableObject<T?> y)
    52	        {
    53	            if (x.IsNull && y.IsNull)
    54	            {
    55	                return true;
    56	            }
    57	
    58	            if (x.IsNull || y.IsNull)
    59	            {
    60	                return false;
    61	            }
    62	
    63	            return ElementComparer.Equals(x.Item, y.Item);
    64	        }
    65	
    66	        public int GetHashCode(NullableObject<T?> obj)
    67	        {
    68	            if (obj.IsNull)
    69	            {
    70	                return 0;
    71	            }
    72	
    73	            return ElementComparer.GetHashCode(obj.Item);
    74	        }
    75	    }
    76	
    77	    /// <summary>
    78	    /// Gets the ordered list of all visible items in the dropdown.
    79	    /// </summary>
    80	    /// <remarks>
    81	    /// Exposed as List to support FindIndex operations in the parent component.
    82	    /// </remarks>
    83	    public IReadOnlyList<MudSelectItem<T>> Items => _items;
    84	
    85	    /// <summary>
    86	    /// Gets all shadow items (including both visible and hidden items).
    87	    /// </summary>
    88	    public IReadOnlyCollection<MudSelectItem<T>> ShadowItems => _shadowLookup.Values;
    89	
    90	    /// <summary>
    91	    /// Gets whether multi-selection is enabled.
    92	    /// </summary>
    93	    public bool MultiSelection => _select.MultiSelection;
    94	
    95	    /// <summary>
    96	    /// Gets the current selected values.
    97	    /// </summary>
    98	    public IReadOnlyCollection<T?> SelectedValues => _select.GetSelectedValues() ?? Array.Empty<T?>();
    99	
   100	    /// <summary>
   101	    /// Gets the user-supplied value comparer from the parent <see cref="MudSelect{T}"/>, if any.
   102	    /// </summary>
   103	    public IEqualityComparer<T?>? Comparer => _select.Comparer;
   104	
   105	    /// <summary>
   106	    /// Rebuilds the internal dictionaries. This should be called when the comparer changes
   107	    /// to ensure hash codes are recalculated with the new comparer.
   108	    /// </summary>
   109	    public void RebuildDictionaries()
   110	    {
   111	        // Rebuild value lookup with the current comparer
   112	        var newValueLookup = new Dictionary<NullableObject<T?>, MudSelectItem<T>>(_comparer);
   113	        foreach (var kvp in _valueLookup)
   114	        {
   115	            newValueLookup[kvp.Key] = kvp.Value;
   116	        }
   117	        _valueLookup = newValueLookup;
   118	
   119	        // Rebuild shadow lookup with the current comparer
   120	        var newShadowLookup = new Dictionary<NullableObject<T?>, MudSelectItem<T>>(_comparer);
   121	        foreach (var kvp in _shadowLookup)
   122	        {
   123	            newShadowLookup[kvp.Key] = kvp.Value;
   124	        }
   125	        _shadowLookup = newShadowLookup;
   126	    }
   127	
   128	    /// <summary>
   129	    /// Registers an item as visible in the dropdown list.
   130	    /// </summary>
   131	    /// <param name="item">The item to register.</param>
   132	    /// <returns><c>true</c> if the item is currently selected; otherwise <c>false</c>.</returns>
   133	    public bool RegisterItem(MudSelectItem<T> item)
   134	    {
   135	        // Add to the ordered list of visible items
   136	        if (!_items.Contains(item))
   137	        {
   138	            _items.Add(item);
   139	        }
   140	
   141	        // Add to value lookup for fast access by value
   142	        _valueLookup[item.Value] = item;
   143	
   144	        // Note: Do NOT add to _shadowLookup here - that's only for shadow items
   145	        // Shadow items are registered separately via RegisterShadowItem
   146	
   147	        // Check if this item's value is currently selected
   148	        var comparer = _select.Comparer ?? EqualityComparer<T?>.Default;
   149	        return _select.MultiSelection switch
   150	        {
   151	            true => _select.GetSelectedValues()?.Contains(item.Value, comparer) == true,
   152	            false => comparer.Equals(_select.ReadValue, item.Value)
   153	        };
   154	    }
   155	
   156	    /// <summary>
   157	    /// Unregisters an item from the dropdown list.
   158	    /// </summary>
   159	    /// <param name="item">The item to unregister.</param>
   160	    public void UnregisterItem(MudSelectItem<T> item)
   161	    {
   162	        _items.Remove(item);
   163	        _valueLookup.Remove(item.Value);
   164	        // Note: Do NOT remove from _shadowLookup - that's managed by shadow items
   165	    }
   166	
   167	    /// <summary>
   168	    /// Registers an item for value-to-RenderFragment lookup only (not visible in dropdown).
   169	    /// </summary>
   170	    /// <remarks>
   171	    /// Used for items with HideContent=true that provide RenderFragments for selected values
   172	    /// that may not be in the visible dropdown list.
   173	    /// </remarks>
   174	    /// <param name="item">The item to register.</param>
   175	    public void RegisterShadowItem(MudSelectItem<T>? item)
   176	    {
   177	        if (item is null)
   178	        {
   179	            return;
   180	        }
   181	
   182	        _shadowLookup[item.Value] = item;
   183	        _select.InvalidateFitContent();
   184	    }
   185	
   186	    /// <summary>
   187	    /// Unregisters a shadow item.
   188	    /// </summary>
   189	    /// <param name="item">The item to unregister.</param>
   190	    public void UnregisterShadowItem(MudSelectItem<T>? item)
   191	    {
   192	        if (item is null)
   193	        {
   194	            return;
   195	        }
   196	
   197	        _shadowLookup.Remove(item.Value);
   198	        _select.InvalidateFitContent();
   199	    }
   200	
   201	    /// <summary>
   202	    /// Updates the visible-item lookup when a registered item's <see cref="MudSelectItem{T}.Value"/> parameter changes.
   203	    /// </summary>
   204	    /// <remarks>
   205	    /// The lookup is keyed by value captured at registration time. When the value parameter is later mutated
   206	    /// (e.g. the parent swaps the underlying data collection while reusing the same component instances),
   207	    /// the old key would otherwise point to a stale <see cref="MudSelectItem{T}"/> reference and the new value
   208	    /// would not be found at all.
   209	    /// </remarks>
   210	    public void OnItemValueChanged(MudSelectItem<T> item, T? oldValue, T? newValue)
   211	    {
   212	        var oldKey = new NullableObject<T?>(oldValue);
   213	        if (_valueLookup.TryGetValue(oldKey, out var existing) && ReferenceEquals(existing, item))
   214	        {
   215	            _valueLookup.Remove(oldKey);
   216	        }
   217	
   218	        _valueLookup[newValue] = item;
   219	    }
   220	
   221	    /// <summary>
   222	    /// Updates the shadow lookup when a registered shadow item's <see cref="MudSelectItem{T}.Value"/> parameter changes.
   223	    /// </summary>
   224	    /// <remarks>
   225	    /// Also requests a re-render of the parent <see cref="MudSelect{T}"/>: <c>GetSelectedValuePresenter</c> runs
   226	    /// during the parent's render pass, before child <c>SetParametersAsync</c> has propagated the new value,
   227	    /// so a second render is needed for the correct <see cref="MudSelectItem{T}.ChildContent"/> to be emitted.
   228	    /// </remarks>
   229	    public void OnShadowItemValueChanged(MudSelectItem<T> item, T? oldValue, T? newValue)
   230	    {
   231	        var oldKey = new NullableObject<T?>(oldValue);
   232	        if (_shadowLookup.TryGetValue(oldKey, out var existing) && ReferenceEquals(existing, item))
   233	        {
   234	            _shadowLookup.Remove(oldKey);
   235	        }
   236	
   237	        _shadowLookup[newValue] = item;
   238	        _select.InvalidateFitContent();
   239	        ((IMudStateHasChanged)_select).StateHasChanged();
   240	    }
   241	
   242	    /// <summary>
   243	    /// Attempts to get an item by its value from visible items.
   244	    /// </summary>
   245	    public bool TryGetItemByValue(T? value, [NotNullWhen(true)] out MudSelectItem<T>? item)
   246	    {
   247	        return _valueLookup.TryGetValue(value, out item);
   248	    }
   249	
   250	    /// <summary>
   251	    /// Attempts to get an item by its value from all items (including shadow items).
   252	    /// </summary>
   253	    public bool TryGetShadowItemByValue(T? value, [NotNullWhen(true)] out MudSelectItem<T>? item)
   254	    {
   255	        return _shadowLookup.TryGetValue(value, out item);
   256	    }
   257	
   258	    /// <summary>
   259	    /// Subscribes to selection changes.
   260	    /// </summary>
   261	    /// <param name="observer">The callback to invoke when selection changes.</param>
   262	    /// <returns>A disposable subscription that can be used to unsubscribe.</returns>
   263	    public IDisposable SubscribeToSelectionChanges(Func<IReadOnlyCollection<T?>, Task> observer)
   264	    {
   265	        _selectionObservers.Add(observer);
   266	        return new SelectionSubscription(this, observer);
   267	    }
   268	
   269	    /// <summary>
   270	    /// Unsubscribes an observer from selection changes.
   271	    /// </summary>
   272	    private void Unsubscribe(Func<IReadOnlyCollection<T?>, Task> observer)
   273	    {
   274	        _selectionObservers.Remove(observer);
   275	    }
   276	
   277	    /// <summary>
   278	    /// Notifies all observers of a selection change.
   279	    /// </summary>
   280	    public async Task NotifySelectionChangedAsync()
   281	    {
   282	        var selectedValues = SelectedValues;
   283	        for (var i = _selectionObservers.Count - 1; i >= 0; i--)
   284	        {
   285	            await _selectionObservers[i](selectedValues);
   286	        }
   287	    }
   288	
   289	    private sealed class SelectionSubscription(MudSelectContext<T> context, Func<IReadOnlyCollection<T?>, Task> observer)
   290	        : IDisposable
   291	    {
   292	        private MudSelectContext<T>? _context = context;
   293	        private Func<IReadOnlyCollection<T?>, Task>? _observer = observer;
   294	
   295	        public void Dispose()
   296	        {
   297	            var contextCopy = _context;
   298	            var observerCopy = _observer;
   299	
   300	            if (contextCopy is null || observerCopy is null)
   301	            {
   302	                return;
   303	            }
   304	
   305	            _context = null;
   306	            _observer = null;
   307	
   308	            contextCopy.Unsubscribe(observerCopy);
   309	        }
   310	    }
   311	}

This is used in the razor template. With my fix, this should now correctly find items using the custom comparer.

Another thing: the `SelectOption` method in `MudSelect.razor.cs`:

```csharp
public async Task SelectOption(T? value)
{
    var comparer = Comparer ?? EqualityComparer<T?>.Default;

    if (MultiSelection)
    {
        // Toggle selection
        if (!_selectedValues.Add(value))
        {
            _selectedValues.Remove(value);
        }
        ...
    }
    else
    {
        ...
        // Early exit if unchanged
        if (comparer.Equals(ReadValue, value))
        {
            await UpdateSelectedValuesStateAsync(comparer);
            return;
        }

        // Replace selection
        _selectedValues.Clear();
        _selectedValues.Add(value);
        ...
    }
    ...
}
```

The `_selectedValues.Add(value)` and `_selectedValues.Remove(value)` rely on the hash set's internal comparer. If `_selectedValues` was properly initialized (via `OnComparerChangedAsync` or `OnSelectedValuesChangedAsync`), it will use the custom comparer. But if neither has been set, it uses default equality.

But this is the same as before my changes - the only difference is that now the lookup dictionaries also respect the custom comparer, which was the main issue.

+        public bool Equals(NullableObject<T?> x, NullableObject<T?> y)
+        {
+            if (x.IsNull && y.IsNull)
+            {
+                return true;
+            }
+
+            if (x.IsNull || y.IsNull)
+            {
+                return false;
+            }
+
+            return ElementComparer.Equals(x.Item, y.Item);
+        }

+        {
+            if (obj.IsNull)
+            {
+                return 0;
+            }
+

+        }

+    {
+        private readonly MudSelect<T> _select;
+
+        public NullableObjectComparer(MudSelect<T> select)
+        {
+            _select = select;
+        }
+
+        private IEqualityComparer<T?> ElementComparer => _select.Comparer ?? EqualityComparer<T?>.Default;
+
+        public bool Equals(NullableObject<T?> x, NullableObject<T?> y)
+        {
+            if (x.IsNull && y.IsNull)
+            {
+                return true;
+            }
+
+            if (x.IsNull || y.IsNull)
+            {
+                return false;
+            }
+
+            return ElementComparer.Equals(x.Item, y.Item);
+        }
+
+        public int GetHashCode(NullableObject<T?> obj)
+        {
+            if (obj.IsNull)
+            {
+                return 0;
+            }
+
+            return ElementComparer.GetHashCode(obj.Item);
+        }
     }

+    public void RebuildDictionaries()
